## Instruction

Update the main product image based on WooCommerce order data, setting the image of the best-selling variation of each product as the main product image.

## Initial State

### WooCommerce

You can review the data construction process during testing [here](https://github.com/hkust-nlp/mcpbench_dev/tree/finalpool_dev/tasks/finalpool/woocommerce-update-cover/preprocess).

<div className="thinking-box">
🧐`Agent`

I'll help you update the main product images based on WooCommerce order data. This involves several steps:

1. First, I'll get the orders data to analyze sales
2. Identify the best-selling variations for each product
3. Update the main product images accordingly

Let me start by getting the orders data and then analyze the sales patterns.

```python 
# Parse the order data
orders1 = json.loads(orders_page1)
orders2 = json.loads(orders_page2)
all_orders = orders1 + orders2

# Analyze sales data by product and variation
product_variations = defaultdict(lambda: defaultdict(int))
variation_images = {}
product_names = {}

for order in all_orders:
    for item in order['line_items']:
        product_id = item['product_id']
        variation_id = item['variation_id']
        quantity = item['quantity']
        
        # Track sales quantities
        product_variations[product_id][variation_id] += quantity
        
        # Store variation image and product name
        variation_images[variation_id] = item['image']
        product_names[product_id] = item['parent_name']

# Find best-selling variation for each product
best_selling_variations = {}
for product_id, variations in product_variations.items():
    best_variation_id = max(variations.items(), key=lambda x: x[1])
    best_selling_variations[product_id] = {
        'variation_id': best_variation_id[0],
        'total_quantity': best_variation_id[1],
        'image': variation_images[best_variation_id[0]],
        'product_name': product_names[product_id]
    }

print("Sales Analysis Results:")
print("=" * 50)

for product_id, data in best_selling_variations.items():
    print(f"\nProduct ID: {product_id}")
    print(f"Product Name: {data['product_name']}")
    print(f"Best-selling Variation ID: {data['variation_id']}")
    print(f"Total Quantity Sold: {data['total_quantity']}")
    print(f"Variation Image: {data['image']['src']}")
    print(f"Image ID: {data['image']['id']}")

print("\n" + "=" * 50)
print("Summary of products to update:")
for product_id, data in best_selling_variations.items():
    print(f"Product {product_id}: Update main image to {data['image']['src']}")
```

```python 
    {"product_id": 32, "variation_id": 33, "quantity": 1, "image_id": 11, "image_src": "test_image_red.jpg", "product_name": "Wireless Bluetooth Headphones"},
    {"product_id": 22, "variation_id": 25, "quantity": 2, "image_id": 15, "image_src": "test_image_green.jpg", "product_name": "Rainbow Sneakers"},
]

# Analyze sales data by product and variation
product_variations = defaultdict(lambda: defaultdict(int))
variation_images = {}
product_names = {}

for order in orders_data:
    product_id = order['product_id']
    variation_id = order['variation_id']
    quantity = order['quantity']
    
    # Track sales quantities
    product_variations[product_id][variation_id] += quantity
    
    # Store variation image and product name
    variation_images[variation_id] = {
        'id': order['image_id'], 
        'src': f"https://localhost:10003/store85/wp-content/uploads/sites/6/2025/09/{order['image_src']}"
    }
    product_names[product_id] = order['product_name']

# Find best-selling variation for each product
best_selling_variations = {}
for product_id, variations in product_variations.items():
    best_variation_id = max(variations.items(), key=lambda x: x[1])
    best_selling_variations[product_id] = {
        'variation_id': best_variation_id[0],
        'total_quantity': best_variation_id[1],
        'image': variation_images[best_variation_id[0]],
        'product_name': product_names[product_id]
    }

print("COMPREHENSIVE SALES ANALYSIS RESULTS:")
print("=" * 60)

for product_id, data in best_selling_variations.items():
    print(f"\nProduct ID: {product_id}")
    print(f"Product Name: {data['product_name']}")
    print(f"Best-selling Variation ID: {data['variation_id']}")
    print(f"Total Quantity Sold: {data['total_quantity']}")
    print(f"Variation Image: {data['image']['src']}")
    print(f"Image ID: {data['image']['id']}")

print("\n" + "=" * 60)
print("SUMMARY - Products to update with best-selling variation images:")
for product_id, data in best_selling_variations.items():
    print(f"Product {product_id}: Set main image to Image ID {data['image']['id']} ({data['image']['src']})")

# Create update plan
update_plan = []
for product_id, data in best_selling_variations.items():
    update_plan.append({
        'product_id': product_id,
        'image_id': data['image']['id'],
        'image_src': data['image']['src']
    })

print(f"\nReady to update {len(update_plan)} products with their best-selling variation images.")
```

```python 
# Summary of completed updates
updates_completed = [
    {
        'product_id': 27,
        'product_name': 'Fashion Backpack',
        'best_selling_variation': 'Blue',
        'new_image': 'test_image_blue.jpg',
        'image_id': 13,
        'total_quantity_sold': 11
    },
    {
        'product_id': 32,
        'product_name': 'Wireless Bluetooth Headphones',
        'best_selling_variation': 'Red',
        'new_image': 'test_image_red.jpg',
        'image_id': 11,
        'total_quantity_sold': 5
    },
    {
        'product_id': 22,
        'product_name': 'Rainbow Sneakers',
        'best_selling_variation': 'Green',
        'new_image': 'test_image_green.jpg',
        'image_id': 15,
        'total_quantity_sold': 7
    }
]

print("🎉 PRODUCT IMAGE UPDATES COMPLETED SUCCESSFULLY!")
print("=" * 65)
print()

for update in updates_completed:
    print(f"✅ Product: {update['product_name']} (ID: {update['product_id']})")
    print(f"   📊 Best-selling variation: {update['best_selling_variation']} ({update['total_quantity_sold']} units sold)")
    print(f"   🖼️  Main image updated to: {update['new_image']} (Image ID: {update['image_id']})")
    print(f"   🔗 Image URL: https://localhost:10003/store85/wp-content/uploads/sites/6/2025/09/{update['new_image']}")
    print()

print("=" * 65)
print("📈 SALES ANALYSIS SUMMARY:")
print(f"• Total products analyzed: {len(updates_completed)}")
print(f"• Total units sold across all best-selling variations: {sum(u['total_quantity_sold'] for u in updates_completed)}")
print()
print("🎯 IMPACT:")
print("• Product main images now showcase the most popular variations")
print("• Customers will see the best-selling color options first")
print("• This should improve conversion rates and customer satisfaction")
print()
print("✨ All product main images have been successfully updated based on sales data!")
```
